That is until she meets a guy named June, who unintentionally becomes her friend and someone she might finally be able to confide in and depend on for help.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mThumb3\"><a href=\"/book/15/CAT_AND_DOG\" class=\"B\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00015/s0/B15_S0_RECTANGLE_M.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">CAT AND DOG</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Hee -Jung Park</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A brooding actor named Seul-Woo and a naïve country girl named Young-Woo were arranged to be married when they were kids. Now adults, the time for their marriage has arrived. OR NOT</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Goeun</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>What happens when a tired old couple is given a second chance to escape their married life and start over? Will they take this opportunity to part ways for good or rekindle a love they never had?</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mThumb2\"><a href=\"/book/15/CAT_AND_DOG\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00015/s0/B15_S0_RECTANGLE_M.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">CAT AND DOG</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Hee -Jung Park</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A brooding actor named Seul-Woo and a naïve country girl named Young-Woo were arranged to be married when they were kids. Now adults, the time for their marriage has arrived. Essentially strangers, the newlyweds must now learn how to deal with living together, clingy exes, betrayal and their own complicated feelings for each other.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mThumb3\"><a href=\"/book/41/THE_SENSUAL_M\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00041/s0/B41_S0_RECTANGLE_M.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">THE SENSUAL M</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Winter</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A seemingly clean cut office worker keeps his BDSM sexual fantasies to himself - until he discovers his co-worker a potential dominatrix…. But fate is cruel and Y-rul and Shio meet again two weeks before her wedding to another man. Their passion and love for each other is evident but the restraints that exist in their current lives as well as the pain of the past, may be too much for them to overcome.  </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"thumb3\"><a href=\"/book/29/MY_BEAUTIFUL_WORLD\" class=\"B\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00029/s0/B29_S0_SQUARE_L.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">MY BEAUTIFUL WORLD</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Maru</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\" stype=\"overflow-y:hidden;\" style=\"height: 90px; overflow: hidden;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p stype=\"height:90px; width:280px; border:1px solid red;\">Ever since she was a child, Yurim Lee has had the ability to literally see the darkness in people. That is until she meets a guy named June, who unintentionally becomes her friend and someone she might finally be able to confide in and depend on for help.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"thumb4\"><a href=\"/book/46/SEE_HEAR_LOVE\" class=\"B\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00046/s0/B46_S0_SQUARE_L.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">SEE, HEAR, LOVE</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Nasty Cat</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\" stype=\"overflow-y:hidden;\" style=\"height: 90px; overflow: hidden;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p stype=\"height:90px; width:280px; border:1px solid red;\">Geun-Su Min was an up and coming comics artist when he began to lose his sight.  Unable to cope with the burdens of being blind and caring for his mom with Alzheimer, he attempts to commit suicide.  He is rescued by Sori Jhun, a deaf girl, who was his avid fan. His only weakness: the intense love he holds for a key-ring figure of his favorite anime character, 'Aris Chan'. One fateful night, a girl appears before him looking just like her - is this fate? Could his beloved 'Aris Chan' have come to life specially for him?</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t</ul></div></div>\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<!-- 모바일용  -->\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"bx-wrapper\" style=\"max-width: 785px; margin: 0px;\"><div class=\"bx-viewport\" style=\"width: 100%; overflow: hidden; position: relative; height: 0px;\"><ul class=\"mListInner\" style=\"width: 415%; position: relative; transition-duration: 0s; transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mPannelType1\" style=\"float: left; list-style: none; position: relative; width: 785px;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mThumb1\"><a href=\"/book/84/MAY_I_SHAKE_YOUR_HAND\" class=\"B\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/02077/s0/B2077_S0_RECTANGLE_M.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">MAY I SHAKE YOUR HAND?</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Linwoo</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Lynn has a special ability where she can foresee the image of the last goodbye if she holds a man's hand. She's on a search to find her last love where she will only be separated by old age. </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"mThumb2\"><a href=\"/book/59/CONFESSION\" class=\"B\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"thumb\"><img src=\"https://image.spottoon.com/webtoon/thumbnail/00059/s0/B59_S0_RECTANGLE_M.jpg\" alt=\"\"></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"listCont\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listTitle\">CONFESSION</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"listUser\">Soo-yeon Won</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"description\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"inner\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A seemly perfect man, Y-rul, decides to become a priest to repent and escape his broken past where he lost his true love, Shio. But fate is cruel and Y-rul and Shio meet again two weeks before her wedding to another man.
